            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Shadow-Shadow Fruit</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Shadow</div>
</div>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div>

<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Shadow</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter with the same name and title, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_455" title="Chapter 455">Chapter 455</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Gecko Moria</b><sup id="cite_ref-c925p4_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925p4-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> is the <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</a> and a former member of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a><sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> who resides on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, the largest ship in the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a>. His bounty is <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>320,000,000, which was frozen until he lost his Warlord position.<sup id="cite_ref-infobox_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infobox-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his youth, Moria served as captain of the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a>, until a vast majority of its members were killed in a fight against <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>. This traumatic event led Moria to seek power through an army of <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a>, constructed by his subordinate, Dr. <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a>.
</p><p>He is the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Saga" title="Thriller Bark Saga">Thriller Bark Saga</a> who stole the shadows of <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> and various other beings with <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a> powers. He is also a major antagonist in the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a> where he took part in the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> and sided with the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, along with most of the other Warlords.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria_at_Marineford_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria_at_Marineford-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the end of the war, he was stripped of his title and was to be eliminated by <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> but he managed to escape into the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-fate_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fate-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> later <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">cloned</a> Moria as one of the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a> to replace the Warlords.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Two years after the war, he attacked the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c925_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> but was defeated and imprisoned when he refused to join Blackbeard.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He was later rescued by <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a> with the help of <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1126_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1126-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Moria is an abnormally large humanoid creature with very distinct, devil-like features.<sup id="cite_ref-described_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-described-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Standing at 692&#160;cm (22'8½") in height, he was the tallest among the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ageandheight_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ageandheight-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He has two horns protruding from the sides of his forehead and stitches running vertically from the top of his face and down his neck, which is rather long and thick in comparison to his body. His ears and teeth are both pointed,<sup id="cite_ref-described_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-described-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> while his lower body is relatively fat and stubby in comparison.<sup id="cite_ref-first_appearance_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first_appearance-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria's hair is extremely short and spiky it's a dark red color (reddish-purple in the anime), and his skin is a pale blue, matching his lips, armbands and the edges of his gloves. His coat and gloves are black, while his pants are bright orange with pale window shapes imprinted on them. He wears a fishnet shirt underneath a cravat, a necklace, and a blue crucifix-like ornament with claw-like appendages sprouting out from three of the cross's points.<sup id="cite_ref-described_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-described-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> During the meeting of the Warlords of the Sea at the <a href="/wiki/Marine_Headquarters" title="Marine Headquarters">Marine Headquarters</a> and later on during/after the war, Moria added a fur-laced cape to his attire.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlords_Meeting_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlords_Meeting-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the timeskip, Moria has switched his cravat and crucifix for a tie with a print of the aforementioned crucifix on it. His coat now has a jagged appearance, and he no longer wears a fishnet undershirt, but a regular shirt with chain-like ornaments in it. He still wears a fur-laced cape, although a much shorter one.
</p><p>During <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s execution twenty-two years before <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> set out on his adventure, Moria looked much thinner, had a pointed chin, and a little longer hair. He also did not have any cross stitches from below his lip, though he did possess them on his forehead.<sup id="cite_ref-Roger&#39;s_Execution_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roger&#39;s_Execution-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> His appearance was similar when he challenged Kaidou in Wano a year later.<sup id="cite_ref-c969_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c969-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/SBS_Volume_63" title="SBS Volume 63">SBS Volume 63</a>, Oda drew the Seven Warlords as children. Moria had shorter horns and hair and was missing the cross stitches running down the middle of his face. He wore a baggy, long-sleeved white shirt with suspenders and dark, knee-high pants. He also wore his usual long black gloves with cowboy boots with spurs and a jewel-encrusted dagger on his belt. He was also much thinner and had a chin and longer legs.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Gecko_Moria_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200113031856" class="image"><img alt="Gecko Moria Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Gecko Moria Portrait.png" data-image-key="Gecko_Moria_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Gecko_Moria_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20200113031856" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">A close up of Moria's face.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20220817233540" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Confronts Moria" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Confronts Moria.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817233540" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20220817233540" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Confronts Moria" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817233540" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Confronts Moria.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817233540" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Confronts_Moria.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria relaxes as Luffy confronts him.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moria has a relaxed, laid-back, and even lazy personality, seemingly appearing to believe he cannot lose.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He also believes that a true pirate should fear nothing, not even death.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Similar to fellow <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a> <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, in most situations Moria is constantly grinning maniacally, and only seems to change expression when something bad happens to him<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> or when he believes his power is being ridiculed.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Like many others, Moria has a <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">distinct style of laughing</a>: "Kishishishi".<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In general, he prefers to avoid fighting altogether, or at least fighting his enemy directly, either making his shadow fight<sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight1_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight1-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight2_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight2-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> or ordering one of his subordinates to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> His proclivity to delegate tasks to his minions is also a weakness in and of itself, along with making exceptions to act out himself should his personal pride or power be questioned; Jinbe noted that Moria had grown weak from his lack of training.<sup id="cite_ref-Weakened_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Weakened-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria desires to become the new <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a> and believes that this is possible to achieve if he has powerful subordinates. Though he once claimed that he would rely on his own powers to achieve his goals,<sup id="cite_ref-Reliance_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reliance-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> he is incredibly lazy; his motto is "relying upon others for one's own objective"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/jp:%E4%BB%96%E5%8A%9B%E6%9C%AC%E9%A1%98" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:jp:他力本願">他力本願</a></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">tarikihongan</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> and his favorite phrase is "You do it!!"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">お前がやれ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Omae ga yare</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-infobox_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infobox-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> This also extends to his fighting style, as he prefers to lay back and let his shadow battle with the powers of the <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight1_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight1-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight2_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight2-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also appears to have considerable knowledge of the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> and how terrifying it is. At Thriller Bark, he told Luffy that with his current strength, he would lose his crew;<sup id="cite_ref-experience_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-experience-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> his prediction came true before the Straw Hats went to the New World, at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-separated_by_Kuma_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-separated_by_Kuma-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria has a lot of experience, having fought many opponents in the past, including an Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-Loss_to_Kaidou_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Loss_to_Kaidou-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He is a good battle tactician, being able to outsmart even <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> However, his overconfidence and laziness made him underestimate his opponents, and ultimately led to his defeat at the hands of the Straw Hat Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-Defeated_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeated-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Even if I had allowed you to continue peacefully on your voyage... At your level, death is all you would have found... You're nowhere near ready for the "New World"...!!! Though it would appear you have gathered yourself quite a fine crew.... You would only lose it all!!![...] My words...come from experience. My subordinates... They were famed, far and wide... Why did I have to lose them all...?!!! My friends were lost to me precisely because they were still alive!!! If they had all been zombies, dead from the start, I would have lost nothing!!! For zombies are invulnerable!! Eternal warriors; even if they are purified, a replacement can be found!!!</td>

  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Moria expresses his beliefs.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
In the past, Moria had the Gecko Pirates who he considered to be valuable comrades, and by his own admission was overconfident and headstrong.<sup id="cite_ref-Reliance_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reliance-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> He also deeply cared for his crewmates, which was a point of tragedy when his last encounter with the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> known as <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> ended with Moria being the sole survivor of his crew. Shell-shocked and traumatized by the horrific event, Moria immediately departed from the New World, and decided that the only way he would not have to face such pain ever again would be to make his comrades unable to suffer by turning them into mindless <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a> that serve only his desires. The loss of his crew to Kaidou changed Moria's outlook on life substantially, making him believe that subordinates are better off as zombies because, due to their undead status, they cannot be harmed by any physical damage - they can only be "purified" by the sea or elements of the sea and even if they were purified, he could easily find other shadows to reanimate them.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> In addition, creating a zombie powerful enough to defeat Kaidou became one of Moria's driving motivations.<sup id="cite_ref-Loss_to_Kaidou_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Loss_to_Kaidou-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his cruelty and twisted outlook on life, he is capable of showing true care towards those close to him. When Absalom was kidnapped by Blackbeard, Moria did not hesitate to go try to rescue him despite the risks of entering an Emperor's territory, especially given how the Blackbeard Pirates are hunting powerful Devil Fruits. He was also shown to be loving towards Perona when she was growing up, as Perona herself viewed Moria as a father figure, suggesting he is capable of displaying affection to others.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_empathy_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_empathy-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crews">Crews</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gecko_Pirates">Gecko Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Moria_Snaps.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816163137" class="image"><img alt="Moria Snaps" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Moria Snaps.png" data-image-key="Moria_Snaps.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Moria_Snaps.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220816163137" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Moria_Snaps.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816163137" class="image"><img alt="Moria Snaps" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Moria_Snaps.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220816163137" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Moria Snaps.png" data-image-key="Moria_Snaps.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Moria_Snaps.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220816163137" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Moria_Snaps.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remembering the fate of his old crew causes Moria to snap.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moria appears to have cared deeply for the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a>, who were famous throughout the world. Upon losing them all in the battle between his crew and the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> at Wano Country, Moria became bitter and his ideals of a crew changed drastically, desiring a crew of <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a> that would never result in another irreplaceable loss. Despite his twisted perceptions, Moria still seems to mourn their loss and even reacts quite heavily when thinking about them.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</a> were very loyal and very respectful to Moria, and always seemed to care about his well-being; however, their loyalties towards Moria seemed to be due to a myriad of reasons. For the zombies, their servitude was mainly fueled by Moria's hold on their very being, granted to him by his <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a> powers.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> As for the humans in his crew, they continued to serve him either due to the deals that Moria seemed to have made with them in the past or their goals coinciding with his at the time (i.e., Perona's desire to be granted servants of her own,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Doctor Hogback's eagerness to breathe life into corpses,<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and Absalom's wish to become the "Graveyard King"<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>).
</p><p>Among the Mysterious Four, <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a> was easily the most dutiful crewmate under Moria, having actively worked for Moria's best interests, such as when he awakened the General Zombies to fight the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> During the Wano Country Arc, it is revealed that Moria also cared about Absalom when he forced his way on to Blackbeard's island in order to rescue Absalom and was beyond relieved when Absalom was supposedly fine but was extremely angered when it was revealed that "Absalom" was actually <a href="/wiki/Catarina_Devon" title="Catarina Devon">Catarina Devon</a> who used her Devil Fruit abilities to trick him and informed him that Absalom was killed by them so <a href="/wiki/Shiryu" title="Shiryu">Shiryu</a> could have Absalom's Devil Fruit.
</p><p>When Moria came to <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a> requesting his assistance in creating an army of the undead to conquer the New World, Hogback agreed on the condition that he would have his late love, <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Cindry" title="Victoria Cindry">Victoria Cindry</a>, resurrected.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Ever since then, Hogback saw Moria as his master, and helped him to create his zombie army and improve Moria's subordinate Absalom's physical strength.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Hogback greatly preferred his position as a pirate's scientist committing blasphemous experiments over being a world-famous surgeon saving people's lives.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Moria's defeat, Hogback and Absalom proved their loyalty by escaping Thriller Bark with an unconscious Moria after he was defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-Escape_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Escape-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a> has been with Moria since she was a child, having been adopted by the latter and raising her as a daughter. While Perona is very close and loving to Moria, Perona's loyalty was somewhat questionable, as she not only attempted to flee when she felt her life was endangered but took all the rations and treasure on board with her.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> However, after receiving news of Moria's supposed death, she appeared to be distraught and lamented his demise.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> When she learned that Moria is alive two years later, Perona was overjoyed and quickly departed Mihawk's castle to go find him.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Buhichuck" title="Buhichuck">Buhichuck</a> was loyal to Moria as well, having tricked some of the Straw Hats into being trapped in a room full of General Zombies.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Gyoro,_Nin,_and_Bao" title="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao">Gyoro, Nin, and Bao</a> seemed to be very scared of Moria, but they were still loyal to him, as they told him when the other members of the Mysterious Four arrived.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Originally, <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a> was very defiant against Moria's will, possessing a strong sense of individuality.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> However, as is the fate of all zombies, Oars eventually became obedient to Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Oars still had his own way of doing things, preferring to fight his battles by himself.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> While Oars allowed Moria to aid him in the execution of his stretching techniques, he was against his master interrupting his battles or fighting them for him.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria, on the other hand, cared very little about most of the <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a> of Thriller Bark; when Absalom informed him that Brook had returned and was slaying zombies, Moria simply insulted him and turned toward another objective with no apparent concern.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> However, he held his human crew in a much higher regard, and was left in shock and despair by their deaths.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Before <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, Moria had already made countless enemies in his search to find powerful underlings, scouring the world for corpses of powerful fighters and shadows to reanimate them, making Moria an enemy of every victim whose shadow he extracted.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nevertheless, in his quest to acquire powerful warriors to support him in his cause, Moria would either steal their shadows<sup id="cite_ref-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> or kill them, but preserve their bodies enough to be converted into suitable zombie warriors.<sup id="cite_ref-Preserving_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Preserving-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Lola" class="mw-redirect" title="Lola">Lola</a> has sworn a grudge against Moria for stealing her and everyone else's shadows, and has remained on Thriller Bark fighting back by purifying zombies and stealing shadows.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> She even mustered the courage to threaten Moria when he was weakened.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria is an enemy of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, who played a pivotal role in defeating him and destroying his army of zombies.<sup id="cite_ref-Defeated_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeated-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> That feeling is mutual, and they also seemed to see each other as rivals, as they both aimed to become the Pirate King.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Moria did acknowledge Luffy's strength, as he chose to use his shadow to empower <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a> in <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At Thriller Bark, he told Luffy that with his current strength, he would lose his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-experience_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-experience-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Not long after that, the Straw Hats did indeed suffer a crushing defeat and separation at the Sabaody Archipelago, thus beginning a training period of two years to prepare themselves for the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-separated_by_Kuma_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-separated_by_Kuma-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, he was angry to see Luffy once again, but took an interest in stealing his shadow again, but Jinbe intervened on Luffy's behalf.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Moria was also the only Warlord of the Sea to be shocked at the revelation of <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a> being Luffy's father.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaidou">Kaidou</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria's apparent biggest enemy is <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, who was responsible for the death of his old crew twenty-three years ago during a clash against the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. Moria spent ten years creating his zombie army to get his revenge against Kaidou, while expressing how much he hated Kaidou for the defeat he suffered back then.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government_and_Marines">World Government and Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite being allied with the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">government</a>, Moria does not care about them. During his time as a Warlord of the Sea, Moria had no problem in stealing <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, pirates, and even civilians' shadows to increase his army of zombies. Moria was furious to learn that the government sent Kuma personally, fearing of Moria's defeat at the hand of the Straw Hats, a fear that would come true. Fearing what would happen if word got out of another Warlord of the Sea falling, the World Government attempted to cover up his defeat by having Kuma kill all of the survivors of Thriller Bark before word got out.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Moria's defeat at Thriller Bark was met with annoyance and disappointment by the World Government, as they had only just replaced <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> after the latter's own defeat and ejection from the Seven Warlords of the Sea.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Even though Kuma chose to disregard the order of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a>, Moria was able to retain his status for a time, later answering the call to arms against the Whitebeard Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlords_Meeting_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlords_Meeting-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the war at Marineford, Moria did not care whether the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and their allies or the Marines won the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, but only thought that Whitebeard's death would be amusing.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, after the war, the World Government finally deemed Moria to be far too weak to continue as a Warlord and decided to annul his pact and eliminate him, under the pretense of Moria dying in the war to preserve the Warlord's reputation of strength.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> However, Moria was able to escape.
</p><p>Moria seems to view the Marines as no different from the pirates and civilians whom he usually extracts shadows from, displaying no qualms about forcibly taking the shadows of nearby Marines to empower himself against Jinbe.<sup id="cite_ref-Shadow_Taking_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shadow_Taking-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> When Doflamingo informed him that he had received orders for Moria's eradication, Moria immediately suspected Sengoku was responsible but was told to think higher up the ranks.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria seems to have had a hostile encounter with <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> in the past, since the latter knows the weakness of Moria's zombie soldiers.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> The two engaged in combat during the Marineford War, with Moria claiming that he would steal Jinbe's shadow. However, the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Men" title="Fish-Men">fish-man</a> landed a powerful hit on him before he could do so<sup id="cite_ref-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> and berated Moria for growing weak because of his refusal to train.<sup id="cite_ref-Weakened_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Weakened-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria was also quite negative toward <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, as Doflamingo damaged <a href="/wiki/Little_Oars_Jr." title="Little Oars Jr.">Little Oars Jr.</a> despite Moria wanting the giant's corpse intact.<sup id="cite_ref-Preserving_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Preserving-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> After the war, he got attacked by Doflamingo, who received orders to kill him. As Moria laid bleeding on the ground, a laughing Doflamingo claimed that he was far too weak to be a Warlord of the Sea and that it would be better for it to look like he died honorably in the war. Even though Moria managed to escape Doflamingo's clutches, Doflamingo was unconcerned, certain that he would die from the wounds he received.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_D._Teach">Marshall D. Teach</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Although they had no interaction when <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> was a Warlord of the Sea, Moria was amused to hear that Blackbeard filled the vacant spot left by Crocodile.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> After the timeskip, Moria showed hostility towards Blackbeard by invading his personal island to rescue <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a> while yelling for Blackbeard to show himself despite him having become an <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>. Even after Moria attacked his underlings, Teach still gave Moria the option to join him, albeit in a mocking tone.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> However, Moria refused and was imprisoned.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_2">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bartholomew_Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria's interactions with <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> have been brief but display an understanding between the two of them. While Moria chastises Kuma for being so loyal to the World Government and not having his own agenda, Kuma showed much patience around Moria, offering to assist him in fighting the Straw Hats despite his disrespect towards him. However, Moria was gravely insulted at his offer and showed no qualms about attacking him, despite Kuma not being affected by his intimidation tactics. Moria also knows about Kuma's <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Nikyu Nikyu no Mi</a> abilities and his habit of asking other people where they would like to go for a vacation before sending the person flying away.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Moria is a former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, as well as one of the most experienced pirates in the entire <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>. In his prime, he was referred to as being a "rival" to <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> (though eventually he lost his entire crew to the man<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>).<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_Rival_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_Rival-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> During the Summit War of Marineford, he was strong enough to battle <a href="/wiki/Curiel" title="Curiel">Curiel</a>, the 10th division commander of the Whitebeard Pirates, while sustaining no injuries<sup id="cite_ref-Battling_Curiel_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Battling_Curiel-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> aside from a strike he suffered from <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> (a fellow former Warlord).<sup id="cite_ref-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> He also managed to fell <a href="/wiki/Little_Oars_Jr." title="Little Oars Jr.">Little Oars Jr.</a> in one move, though others had already injured the mighty giant beforehand.<sup id="cite_ref-Tsuno-Tokage_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tsuno-Tokage-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unfortunately, his tendency to heavily rely on underlings (or his own shadow) to fight for him in the battlefield may have contributed to his diminished prowess in single combat; often, Moria would run away from or ignore an adversary if he deemed the battle as "pointless", as seen when he dismissed Luffy's challenge on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a> because he had already extracted the Straw Hat's shadow from him.<sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight1_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight1-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Jinbe claimed that Moria's dependence on absorbing the shadows of other people had weakened him.<sup id="cite_ref-Weakened_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Weakened-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the Summit War of Marineford ended, <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> claimed that the government had deemed Moria to be far too weak to continue to bear the title of Warlord of the Sea and that he was better off eliminated;<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> despite this, <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Mihawk</a> recalls that Moria was perfectly fine at the end of the war,<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> it still took Doflamingo and a group of <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifistas</a> to corner him,<sup id="cite_ref-fate_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fate-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and Moria still managed to escape (though that was mostly thanks to Absalom).<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As further testament to his potential, Blackbeard, who is known for refusing to recruit weaklings into his crew,<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> asked Moria to become his subordinate.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria has a very strong will, which allowed him to sustain 1000 shadows within his body by using Shadow's Asgard,<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> though it did exert him greatly.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> He was also completely unaffected by a burst of Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>True to his large size and mass, Moria has great strength; he effortlessly lifted a grown man with a single hand while squeezing him hard to enough to make him cough up blood.<sup id="cite_ref-c925p4_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925p4-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> In spite of his physique, however, Moria is incredibly fast: he outran Luffy, who is both much smaller and more accustomed to physical movement, for a considerable amount of time.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria possesses considerable endurance, having gotten up immediately after <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Techniques">attacks</a> by <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi#Nightmare_Luffy" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Nightmare Luffy</a> that toppled <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> and quickly recovered from a powerful strike from <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a><sup id="cite_ref-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria_72-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> to battle a commander of the Whitebeard Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-Battling_Curiel_76-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Battling_Curiel-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> He is also fairly durable, as he did not take any damage when <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Art_of_Weather/Clima-Tact#Techniques" title="Art of Weather/Clima-Tact"><b>Thunderbolt Tempo</b></a> struck Oars.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Also, even though he was crushed under the main tower of Thriller Bark,<sup id="cite_ref-Defeated_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeated-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> only a small injury to his head remained after his recovery, as evidenced by his appearance at Marineford.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlords_Meeting_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlords_Meeting-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Moria is smart and strategic, demonstrating keen planning on multiple occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-Switch_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Switch-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> He often plans ahead with his zombies, placing certain shadows in certain bodies<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> and altering the bodies to suit whatever his purpose would be under the circumstances.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> He apparently knows of the mechanics behind <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>'s ability to transport people elsewhere instantly, something that most people are not even aware of.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Doppelman.png/revision/latest?cb=20220817235126" class="image"><img alt="Doppelman" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Doppelman.png" data-image-key="Doppelman.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Doppelman.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817235126" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Doppelman.png/revision/latest?cb=20220817235126" class="image"><img alt="Doppelman" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Doppelman.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817235126" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Doppelman.png" data-image-key="Doppelman.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3c/Doppelman.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220817235126" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Doppelman.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Doppelman, Moria's shadow clone, formed by his Kage Kage no Mi powers.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moria ate the Kage Kage no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to manifest and control shadows as physical entities. Moria can manifest his own shadow and have it fight in his place, as well as split his shadow into a number of bat-like creatures that he can use to swarm his enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight1_29-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight1-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DoppelFight2_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoppelFight2-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He can also instantaneously swap locations with his shadow.<sup id="cite_ref-Switch_88-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Switch-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> His shadow cannot be destroyed, and it will simply reform if it gets taken down.
</p><p>As a basic law for nature, the body and the shadow are always the same shape. Normally, the shadow is slave to the body, but Moria can put the reverse into practice. By altering the shape of a shadow, he can change the shape of the body.
</p><p>Moria can steal other people's shadows by cutting them off of the owner's body. People who have their shadow stolen are left in a coma for about two days.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, once someone's shadow has been stolen, sunlight becomes deadly to them, reducing them to ashes almost instantly if they are exposed to it.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Victims of shadow theft also lose their reflection and don't appear in a photograph.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> The body and the shadow count as a single being, even when separated; this means that if the person dies, then the shadow will die with them.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> When stolen shadows are released, they automatically fly back to their original owners.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024001" class="image"><img alt="Soldier Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Soldier Zombies.png" data-image-key="Soldier_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024001" class="image"><img alt="Soldier Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Soldier Zombies.png" data-image-key="Soldier_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Soldier_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dead bodies infused with shadows and reanimated into zombies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
