<p>The stolen shadows can be inserted into corpses, reanimating the corpse into a <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombie</a> loyal to Moria, with the shadow serving as its <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> When reanimating a zombie, the physical strength comes from the corpse itself, while the personality and fighting techniques come from the shadow and are identical to those of the shadow's original owner. When both of these elements are strong, it results in a more powerful zombie. Since zombies are already dead, they cannot be killed. As long as they still have their stolen shadow, they'll just keep getting back up. Zombies also never get tired and don't feel pain.
</p><p>Moria can also insert stolen shadows into his own body, causing him to become bigger and stronger. The more shadows he takes in, the more gigantic he becomes, though it also makes him lumbering and uncoordinated, so it's less of a trump card and more of a desperate last resort.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> Shadows can also be placed into the bodies of other living people, increasing their physical power and granting them the ability to use the fighting techniques of the shadow's original owner. However, since a living body already has a soul residing inside it, a shadow placed within a living body will only remain for 10 minutes. After that, the shadow will leave and fly back to its owner.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Moria wields a giant pair of scissors, which he uses in conjuncture with his Kage Kage no Mi to sever people's shadows.<sup id="cite_ref-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow_28-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy&#39;s_Shadow-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He carries these with him all the time so he can steal shadows even during battle, such as when he took Robin's shadow.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The scissor blades can be disconnected at the joint, becoming two inverted swords for Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> With shadows of capable swordsmen implanted into himself, Moria can become a swordsman with dual swords.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is also seen with a sword during his battle against the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c969_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c969-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Moria%27s_Scissors.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428213825" class="image"><img alt="Moria&#39;s Scissors" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="84" data-image-name="Moria&#39;s Scissors.png" data-image-key="Moria%27s_Scissors.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Moria%27s_Scissors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20200428213825" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: left;">Moria using his scissors to sever shadows.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Moria%27s_Scissors_As_a_Pair_of_Swords.png/revision/latest?cb=20160814210320" class="image"><img alt="Moria&#39;s Scissors As a Pair of Swords" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="88" data-image-name="Moria&#39;s Scissors As a Pair of Swords.png" data-image-key="Moria%27s_Scissors_As_a_Pair_of_Swords.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Moria%27s_Scissors_As_a_Pair_of_Swords.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20160814210320" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: left;">Moria's scissors as a pair of swords.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Gecko_Pirates_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20210425042041" class="image"><img alt="Gecko Pirates Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="84" data-image-name="Gecko Pirates Infobox.png" data-image-key="Gecko_Pirates_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Gecko_Pirates_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20210425042041" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: left;">Moria using a sword.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Years">Early Years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">My words... come from experience. My subordinates... they were famed far and wide... Why did I have to lose them all?!!! 
</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Part of Moria's speech on the use of Zombies over real crewmates.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>At age 26, upon travelling to <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a>, Moria attended the planned execution of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, during which he listened to Roger's speech about his treasure <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>, which presumably contributed to his dream of becoming the new Pirate King. After the execution he, like many others, raised his flag and started to make a name for himself in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Roger&#39;s_Execution_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roger&#39;s_Execution-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314031242" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Gecko Moria" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Gecko Moria.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230314031242" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314031242" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Gecko Moria" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230314031242" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Gecko Moria.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230314031242" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_vs_Gecko_Moria.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria clashing with Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A year later, while Moria had a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>320,000,000,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a> clashed with the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> in the Ringo region of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano</a>, during which Moria stole <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Ryuma" title="Shimotsuki Ryuma">Ryuma</a>'s corpse along with <a href="/wiki/Shusui" title="Shusui">Shusui</a> from his grave.<sup id="cite_ref-c969_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c969-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The battle resulted in Moria's entire crew being killed in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-Loss_to_Kaidou_37-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Loss_to_Kaidou-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Following his defeat, Moria set about trying to gain enough power to defeat <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Loss_to_Kaidou_37-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Loss_to_Kaidou-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> and his outlook of crewmates led to him seeking an undead crew.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria&#39;s_loss_4-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria&#39;s_loss-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Returning to his home sea of <a href="/wiki/West_Blue" title="West Blue">West Blue</a>, he constructed <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, and some time afterwards joined the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> resulting in his bounty being frozen. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew_Reformation">Crew Reformation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724013007" class="image"><img alt="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona.png" data-image-key="Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724013007" class="image"><img alt="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona.png" data-image-key="Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hogback_Meets_Moria,_Absalom_and_Perona.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria meets Hogback.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At an unknown point, Moria accepted <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</a> and also found a child named <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a>, who he chose to take in and raise as his own, leading to her eventually seeing him as a father figure.<sup id="cite_ref-SBSChild_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SBSChild-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> Later, at age 38, the crew met <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a>. Upon encountering the doctor, Moria offered him a way to bring his deceased love, <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Cindry" title="Victoria Cindry">Victoria Cindry</a>, back to life. Through the use of his Devil Fruit powers, Moria implanted a stolen shadow into the corpse and gained the doctor's allegiance in return.<sup id="cite_ref-Past_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In order to build an army, Moria stole corpses from across the world including <a href="/wiki/John" title="John">John</a>, Ryuma, and <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Ice" title="Land of Ice">Land of Ice</a>. He stored them in Thriller Park in order for Hogback to transform into <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Situating Thriller Park in the the <a href="/wiki/Florian_Triangle" title="Florian Triangle">Florian Triangle</a>, the crew ambushed anyone who entered, looking for those with strong shadows, such as pirates with high bounties, and Moria started making zombie minions with shadows stolen from his victims and creations supplied by Hogback.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Five years ago, a skeleton named <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> came to Thriller Bark in hopes of fixing the rudder to his ship. He was captured and Moria implanted his shadow into the corpse of <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Ryuma" title="Shimotsuki Ryuma">Ryuma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> However, Brook returned to Thriller Bark shortly afterward and purified several of Moria's zombie minions in an attempt to retrieve his shadow. Though Brook was defeated by Ryuma, Moria was forced to rebuild his army from the mess he left behind.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Three and a half years ago, While Moria was laying in bed he learned news from <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a> that a man named <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> was elected as the new member of the Seven Warlords of the Sea, to which he laughed at his "Paw Palmed" moniker. Perona still belived the man must be strong enough to be a warlord. <sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Saga">Thriller Bark Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After four days of sleep, Moria was awoken by his servants and told of the night attack to be commenced on the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, which he then prepared for.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png/revision/latest?cb=20220818015408" class="image"><img alt="Moria Cuts Luffy&#39;s Shadow" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Moria Cuts Luffy&#39;s Shadow.png" data-image-key="Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220818015408" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png/revision/latest?cb=20220818015408" class="image"><img alt="Moria Cuts Luffy&#39;s Shadow" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220818015408" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Moria Cuts Luffy&#39;s Shadow.png" data-image-key="Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220818015408" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Moria_Cuts_Luffy%27s_Shadow.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria cuts Luffy's shadow.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the attack commenced, Moria took <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>'s shadows as they were brought before him, implanting them in the zombies <a href="/wiki/Inuppe" title="Inuppe">Inuppe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jigoro" title="Jigoro">Jigoro</a>, respectively. <sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Later, Luffy was brought to Moria, who expressed his desire to become the Pirate King. After noting that they had only caught Zoro and Sanji prior to obtaining Luffy, Moria berated his subordinates for bickering among themselves over the other Straw Hats escaping and reminded them that he had brought them here to witness the birth of an exceptionally powerful zombie. Luffy attempted to escape but was incapacitated by Perona's <a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a>, allowing Moria to cut off his shadow. <sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Noting that obtaining Luffy's shadow had put him one step closer to becoming the Pirate King, Moria proclaimed that he would not have lost to Kaidou in the New World if he had possessed such a powerful underling before ordering Gyoro, Nin, and Bao to open the door to the special freezer. When Absalom informed him that Brook had returned and was purifying the zombies once more, Moria merely told him to do something about it himself. Soon afterward, Moria, Hogback, Absalom, Perona, and <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a> walked down the hall to the special freezer, with Moria listening to Hogback explaining the legend of the being whose corpse he found in the ice country before stating that they would revive that legend as the group reached the corpse of <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria approached Oars's corpse before informing Luffy's shadow that he was its new master. When Moria explained how he would give it a body and ordered it to forget its past and become his soldier, the shadow nodded its head, prompting Moria to note that the contract was complete before shoving the shadow into Oars's corpse. After a few seconds, Oars began moving and roared, prompting <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a> to fall out of Kumashi, which Moria noticed and was confused by. However, Moria quickly turned his attention back to Oars, whom he noted with delight was easily ripping off his large chains.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While his zombie minions brought in large amounts of food to satisfy Oars's hunger, Moria explained to Oars how he was a legendary villain from five hundred years ago who was revived to become Moria's underling. However, Oars refused to serve Moria and broke out of the freezer as a grinning Moria watched.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After being informed of Oars climbing up Thriller Bark's mast, Moria noted that they will be able to obtain the shadows of even stronger people and create more special zombies before informing Hogback that they would be needing more <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">marios</a>. When <a href="/wiki/Hildon" title="Hildon">Hildon</a> arrived and informed Hogback of Luffy, Zoro, and Sanji waking up and learning how to purify zombies, Moria listened with interest, but was left disappointed when Hogback told him that everything was fine after Perona claimed that she would deal with them herself. Sitting down, Moria told Hogback that he would stay there and play with Oars for a bit.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Soon afterward, Moria was confronted by Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> When Luffy demanded that Moria give back the shadows he had taken and threatened to beat him up in order to make him do so, Moria explained that the shadows would only to return to their owners if he commanded them to do so and that he would need to be severely weakened in order to do this, though he did not believe that Luffy would even be able to touch him at his current level of power. Having Doppelman block Luffy's subsequent attack, Moria admitted that he once aspired to become stronger before claiming that he would become the Pirate King through the strength of others. When Luffy proclaimed that he would be the one to become the Pirate King, Moria noted that Oars said the same thing and that Luffy's will was strong in him before revealing that Oars would eventually lose his memories of being Luffy and become completely obedient toward him. Moria proceeded to attack Luffy with Brick Bat while claiming that an inexperienced brat who underestimates others will only be embarrassed in the end. However, Luffy suddenly jumped off the observation deck and kicked Moria from below, angering him.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Eventually, Oars returned, and Moria confirmed that he had become obedient to him before ordering him to mercilessly attack the Straw Hats and transport the survivors to their ship. After telling Oars to display all of his power, Moria ran away, prompting Luffy to pursue him.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> While continuing to run, Moria taunted Luffy by proclaiming that his crewmates would be falling victim to his fighting prowess while Luffy was chasing him.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> Eventually, Luffy seemingly caught up with Moria and tackled him, only to discover that it was actually Doppelman,<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> which quickly returned to Moria himself.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816161549" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Moria Meet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma and Moria Meet.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816161549" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816161549" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Moria Meet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816161549" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma and Moria Meet.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816161549" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_and_Moria_Meet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma informs Moria of Crocodile's new replacement, Marshall D. Teach.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Thriller Bark began moving out of the Florian Triangle due to Oars fooling around with the rudder, Gyoro, Nin, and Bao informed Moria, who merely claimed that he did not care as long as they remained on the ocean before turning his attention to his newly arrived guest, <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>. Identifying Kuma as being the only Warlord of the Sea who followed the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s every order without question, Moria claimed that he was very ominous because his intentions were mysterious before interpreting Kuma's inquiry of where he would like to go on a trip as a challenge to battle. Kuma revealed that he had come to inform Moria of the appointment of <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>'s successor in the Seven Warlords, <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>, otherwise known as Blackbeard. Upon learning that Blackbeard's former bounty was <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>0, Moria noted that he had done well for the World Government to recognize him before stating that this would restore the world's balance. However, Kuma disagreed and revealed that the World Government was afraid that another Warlord of the Sea would be defeated by the Straw Hats, greatly angering Moria, who was only further enraged when Kuma offered to help him fight the Straw Hats. Demanding to know if Kuma believed he would be defeated by this rookie crew, Moria told him to inform the World Government that the pirate crew that outwitted them were easily made into loyal zombies.
</p><p>Soon afterward, Moria entered the cockpit within Oars's stomach and noted that the night air was refreshing before asking the shocked Straw Hats if they could really afford to waste time with the dawn approaching. Offering the Straw Hats a chance to fight him, Moria explained that they would be able to free all the shadows if they beat him before pointing out that they would not be able to reach him if they did not beat Oars first. When Usopp attempted to enter the ship's kitchen in order to find more salt, Moria had Oars smash his fist into Usopp and the entrance of the mansion, only for Usopp to be rescued by Brook, who had brought a large bag of salt.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Moria promised that he was not a mere passenger and that he would show the Straw Hats their worst nightmare, Oars cried out in pain from being burned, which prompted Moria to remind him that the pain he felt was merely a lingering reaction from when he was human before ordering him to put out the fire. When <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> attempted to attack Moria directly with his mortar, Oars moved himself and Moria out of the way before smashing Franky into a nearby building, prompting Moria to gleefully order him to finish Franky off. When Nami arrived, Oars managed to stretch his arm while attacking her, leading <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> to realize that Moria did something upon noticing him laughing.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After making Oars's limbs stretch when he used <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Techniques#Other_Concepts_and_Themed_Attacks" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Techniques"><i>Gomu Gomu no Kane</i></a> and <i>Gomu Gomu no Spear</i>, Moria revealed that he was using <i>Kage Kakumei</i> to change the shape of Oars's shadow and thus his body, which is what allowed his body to stretch. When Moria demonstrated that Oars was not limited to simply stretching like rubber by turning his body into a sphere for Oars Ball, Oars asked him to not interfere with his fight, which prompted Moria to apologize and explain that he only wanted to help before ordering Oars to crush the Straw Hats one by one. However, after the Straw Hats managed to inflict a severe injury on Oars's right arm, Moria was prevented from allowing him to stretch by <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>, who physically restrained him with <a href="/wiki/Hana_Hana_no_Mi#Arms" title="Hana Hana no Mi"><i>Ochenta Fleur: Cuatro Manos: Hold</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Admitting that Robin's restraints hurt, Moria asked her if she really thought this would stop him before having Doppelman rise from Oars's shadow and using Brick Bat, which injured Robin and knocked her down. When Moria had Doppelman appear behind Robin in preparation for a long-range battle, Robin attempted to break his neck with <i>Cuatro Mano: Clutch</i>, only for Moria to evade the attack by switching places with Doppelman before cutting off Robin's shadow with his scissors. As Moria noted that he did not have a zombie to put Robin's shadow into and that he would simply have to hold onto her for the time being, Sanji attacked him with <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Diable_Jambe#Before_the_Timeskip" title="Black Leg Style/Diable Jambe"><i>Diable Jambe: Extra Hachis</i></a>, but Moria switched places with Doppelman once more to return to Oars's cockpit and apologized for leaving to have a little fun. After Oars pummeled Sanji and Chopper with <i>Gomu Gomu no Gatling</i>, Moria gleefully noted that there were only three targets left. <sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria ordered Oars to crush the remaining three targets. When Usopp shot a large bag of salt into Oars's mouth in an attempt to purify him, Moria had Doppelman catch the bag and throw it back at Usopp, whom he asked if he did not think Moria would be prepared to counter his zombies' weaknesses. As Oars began stomping on Usopp and Nami, Moria enthusiastically encouraged him while proclaiming that he did not want to be able to identify the Straw Hats as human anymore when Oars was done. However, he was interrupted when Nightmare Luffy appeared, having rescued Nami and Usopp. Wondering if Luffy had the power to transform or if he had absorbed shadows, Moria ordered Oars to destroy him, but was shocked when Luffy stopped Oars's <i>Gomu Gomu no Rifle</i> before proceeding to punch Oars back and slam him into the ground with Moria still inside.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Luffy continued to toss Oars around, a battered Moria wondered what was going on and called Oars pathetic for being beaten up by a lone pirate before wondering if he should leave the cockpit again. However, he was interrupted by Luffy, who punched him in the face with <i>Gomu Gomu no Pistol</i> before unleashing a barrage of punches on both him and Oars with <i>Gomu Gomu no Storm</i>, causing Oars to crash into the mansion and seemingly knocking out Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Shadow%27s_Asgard.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816164018" class="image"><img alt="Shadow&#39;s Asgard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shadow&#39;s Asgard.png" data-image-key="Shadow%27s_Asgard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Shadow%27s_Asgard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816164018" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Shadow%27s_Asgard.png/revision/latest?cb=20220816164018" class="image"><img alt="Shadow&#39;s Asgard" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Shadow%27s_Asgard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816164018" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shadow&#39;s Asgard.png" data-image-key="Shadow%27s_Asgard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Shadow%27s_Asgard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220816164018" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shadow%27s_Asgard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria uses <b>Shadow's Asgard</b>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Luffy defeated Oars by shattering his spine, Moria emerged from the cockpit and, upon seeing the <a href="/wiki/Rolling_Pirates" title="Rolling Pirates">Rolling Pirates</a>, noted that he now understood how the now-normal Luffy obtained his powerup while refusing to back down from the fight. Noting that Luffy and his crew were not yet strong enough for the New World, Moria proclaimed that Luffy would lose his entire crew like he did and that he only lost his subordinates because they were alive as black tendrils spread out from him across the ground to the zombies nearby. Activating Shadow's Asgard, Moria proceeded to remove the shadows of one thousand zombies and place them in his own body, resulting in him growing to an enormous and misshapen form, before splitting Thriller Bark in half with a single punch. Seeing this, the Straw Hats got up to confront Moria one last time.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Moria struck at Luffy several times, but the latter managed to evade him due to the speed of <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Gear 2</a>. When Luffy hit him with <i>Gomu Gomu no Jet Rocket</i> and <i>Gomu Gomu no Jet Bazooka</i>, Moria spit up dozens of shadows due to being unable to fully control all of them, prompting him to trap Luffy with Black Box before smashing the box into a wall. When the crumpled box fell on the ground, Moria stomped on it while claiming that this was Luffy's baptism for not knowing his place by defying a Warlord of the Sea. However, Luffy merely broke out of the box and claimed that he would not be crushed by the world because he was made of rubber, angering Moria, before inflating his body with <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Gear 3</a> in order to hit Moria with <i>Gomu Gomu no Gigant Jet Shell</i>, causing him to spit up even more shadows. Refusing to let his soldiers go, Moria clasped his hands over his mouth in an attempt to keep the shadows in, but Luffy hit him with <i>Gomu Gomu no Gigant Jet Shell</i> once more, forcing Moria back into the main mast with such force that it toppled over and fell on him. Finally defeated, Moria told Luffy to go forth and see the real terror of the New World before losing consciousness as the rest of the shadows left his body.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Hogback and Absalom rescued the still unconscious Moria and left Thriller Bark with him on a separate ship.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Amazon_Lily_Arc">Amazon Lily Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When the World Government called upon the Seven Warlords of the Sea to help them battle Whitebeard and his allies, Moria answered the call and dined alongside all of his fellow Warlords save for <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlords_Meeting_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlords_Meeting-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Moria was present at Marineford alongside <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>, <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>, ready for the battle ahead.<sup id="cite_ref-Moria_at_Marineford_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria_at_Marineford-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He was surprised to learn that <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> was <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Roger</a>'s son.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon discovering that <a href="/wiki/Little_Oars_Jr." title="Little Oars Jr.">Little Oars Jr.</a> is under the command of <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, Moria expressed an interest in taking the giant's corpse.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> When Doflamingo cut off Little Oars Jr.'s right leg, an angered Moria decided to demonstrate how to finish him off properly by impaling the giant with <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi#Usage" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Tsuno-Tokage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Tsuno-Tokage_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tsuno-Tokage-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Marineford_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130217151935" class="image"><img alt="Marineford Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marineford Zombies.png" data-image-key="Marineford_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Marineford_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217151935" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Marineford_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130217151935" class="image"><img alt="Marineford Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Marineford_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217151935" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marineford Zombies.png" data-image-key="Marineford_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Marineford_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217151935" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marineford_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria summons his army of Marine zombies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Luffy and his fellow <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> escapees fell from the sky and onto the battlefield, an enraged Moria screamed Luffy's title.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> Wanting to use Luffy's shadow to reanimate Little Oars Jr., Moria attempted to have his zombies fight Luffy, only for <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> to splash them with saltwater and reduce them to lifeless bodies. Immediately afterward, Moria was shocked to learn that Luffy was the son of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Revolutionary Dragon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png/revision/latest?cb=20231011203125" class="image"><img alt="Jinbe Punches Moria With Samegawara Seiken" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jinbe Punches Moria With Samegawara Seiken.png" data-image-key="Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011203125" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png/revision/latest?cb=20231011203125" class="image"><img alt="Jinbe Punches Moria With Samegawara Seiken" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011203125" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jinbe Punches Moria With Samegawara Seiken.png" data-image-key="Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011203125" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jinbe_Punches_Moria_With_Samegawara_Seiken.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jinbe lands a powerful blow on Moria.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moria decided to fight Jinbe head-on and absorbed several shadows in order to empower himself, but Jinbe took him down with a single strike.<sup id="cite_ref-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria_72-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jinbe_Defeats_Moria-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Later, Moria provoked the Whitebeard Pirates' 10th Division Captain <a href="/wiki/Curiel" title="Curiel">Curiel</a> into a fight on the battlefield by stating that he would enjoy seeing Whitebeard die during the war.<sup id="cite_ref-Battling_Curiel_76-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Battling_Curiel-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> When Whitebeard was stabbed by <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a>, Moria reacted with visible joy.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the plaza, Moria fought the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and their allies until Whitebeard created a fissure to separate the pirates and the marines.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> When Whitebeard met his end at the hands of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, Moria merely smiled while watching.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> arrived with the purpose of bringing the war to an end, Moria continued to grin. When <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> called the war off, Moria stood down along with the rest of the Warlords and Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e3/Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png/revision/latest?cb=20220911131250" class="image"><img alt="Moria Attacked by Doflamingo and Pacifistas" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Moria Attacked by Doflamingo and Pacifistas.png" data-image-key="Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e3/Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220911131250" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e3/Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png/revision/latest?cb=20220911131250" class="image"><img alt="Moria Attacked by Doflamingo and Pacifistas" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e3/Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220911131250" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Moria Attacked by Doflamingo and Pacifistas.png" data-image-key="Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e3/Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220911131250" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Moria_Attacked_by_Doflamingo_and_Pacifistas.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Doflamingo and a squad of Pacifistas attempting to kill Moria.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the war, Moria was brutally attacked by Doflamingo and a group of Pacifista in the backstreets of Marineford because, according to Doflamingo, Moria was deemed to be far too weak to continue serving as a Warlord of the Sea and was to be eliminated there with the world believing him to have died in the war. When Moria asked him if the order was from Sengoku, Doflamingo merely grinned and revealed that it came from even higher up.<sup id="cite_ref-Warlord_title_revoked_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Warlord_title_revoked-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Both Absalom and Hogback rescued Moria from Doflamingo's attack at some point.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Perona later read a newspaper article claiming that he died in the war, though Mihawk questioned the validity of this due to recalling that Moria was alive at the end of the battle. Later, while discussing the incident with a member of the World Government, Doflamingo revealed that Moria disappeared before he could deliver the killing blow and wondered if Moria's <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> ability could be the cause of his disappearance, though his interlocutor had doubts about this. Nonetheless, Doflamingo affirmed that Moria was critically injured and would die no matter what he did.<sup id="cite_ref-fate_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fate-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Despite Doflamingo's assertions, several people have reported they have seen Moria alive, and he was in hiding somewhere in the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302155055" class="image"><img alt="Moria Invades Hachinosu" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Moria Invades Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302155055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302155055" class="image"><img alt="Moria Invades Hachinosu" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302155055" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Moria Invades Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230302155055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Moria_Invades_Hachinosu.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Moria rampaging on Hachinosu.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moria and his zombie army went on a rampage on <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard" class="mw-redirect" title="Blackbeard">Blackbeard</a>'s island <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> with Moria demanding for Blackbeard while also searching for Absalom. Moria was relieved when he thought he saw Absalom (actually <a href="/wiki/Catarina_Devon" title="Catarina Devon">Catarina Devon</a> <a href="/wiki/Inu_Inu_no_Mi,_Model:_Kyubi_no_Kitsune" title="Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Kyubi no Kitsune">in disguise</a>) safe and sound, but he was then struck from behind by an invisible <a href="/wiki/Shiryu" title="Shiryu">Shiryu</a>, and Moria was shocked that Shiryu used Absalom's power. Moria was then furious when Devon revealed herself and stated that Absalom was killed. Moria then heard Blackbeard's voice on a loudspeaker, inviting him to join his crew while also mentioning the morning newspaper.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> However, Moria refused and was imprisoned along with other prisoners.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Slightly prior to the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>' raid of Hachinosu, <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a> infiltrated the island's prison and freed <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> in exchange for his help in freeing Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Pizarro</a> later confirmed to <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> that Moria had escaped.<sup id="cite_ref-c1126_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1126-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 222px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Early_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404101559" class="image"><img alt="Early Moria" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="118" height="200" data-image-name="Early Moria.png" data-image-key="Early_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Early_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/118?cb=20150404101559" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Some early concepts of Moria and Perona.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 222px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Early_Shichibukai.png/revision/latest?cb=20150403175321" class="image"><img alt="Early Shichibukai" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="136" height="200" data-image-name="Early Shichibukai.png" data-image-key="Early_Shichibukai.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Early_Shichibukai.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/136?cb=20150403175321" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">An early concept of the Warlords of the Sea members (from left to right: Mihawk, Doflamingo, Moria).
</div></span></div>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a></i>, early concepts of Moria were revealed, showing how he underwent many transformations before becoming his official appearance. One picture shows an early concept of Moria that looks nothing like his current look, with him wearing a strange mask and a hood. The other shows how first, Moria was supposed to be a pastor who had a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dissociative_identity_disorder" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dissociative identity disorder">split personality</a>, and even after his appearance became closer to that of what he is now, his setting was a schemer that sets traps. <sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>His name is spelled "<b>Gekko Moriah</b>" in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a> and the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Exhibition" title="One Piece Exhibition">One Piece Exhibition</a>. However, <a href="/wiki/Chapter_925" title="Chapter 925">Chapter 925</a> Romanized it as "<b>Gecko Moria</b>".<sup id="cite_ref-c925p4_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925p4-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>An old <a href="/wiki/Mythbusters/Misunderstandings_and_Misinformation#Moria.27s_nickname_is_King_of_the_Depths" title="Mythbusters/Misunderstandings and Misinformation">misconception</a> among fans is that Moria's <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a> is believed to be "King of the Depths". In reality, the full name for the Seven Warlords of the Sea is "Below King Seven Armed Seas". It was the "Below King" part that caused confusion to many people, thus giving the impression that "Below King", or "King of the Depths", is his nickname.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Difference">Anime and Manga Difference</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the anime, Jinbe claimed that Moria's dependence on absorbing other people's shadow does not actually make him stronger.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/DXMoria.png/revision/latest?cb=20130217150853" class="image"><img alt="DXMoria" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="292" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DXMoria.png" data-image-key="DXMoria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/DXMoria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217150853" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/DXMoria.png/revision/latest?cb=20130217150853" class="image"><img alt="DXMoria" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/DXMoria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217150853" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="292" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DXMoria.png" data-image-key="DXMoria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/DXMoria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130217150853" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DXMoria.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">One Piece DX Gecko Moria figure.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a prominent character, he has been featured in the fan merchandise. Moria has been featured with the Seven Warlords of the Sea in the series of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Seven_Warlords_Cellphone_Strap" title="One Piece Seven Warlords Cellphone Strap">One Piece Seven Warlords Cellphone Strap</a> and twice in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Deformed_Figures" title="One Piece Super Deformed Figures">One Piece Super Deformed Figures</a>. He was recently released in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_DX_Figure" title="One Piece DX Figure">One Piece DX Figure</a> models. He was released in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_World_Collectable_Figure" title="One Piece World Collectable Figure">One Piece World Collectable Figure</a> series in July 2010 along with the rest of the Warlords.
</p>
