<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_4" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGecko_Moria%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>At Thriller Bark, he told <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> that with his current strength, he would lose his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-experience_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-experience-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Not long after that, the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> did indeed suffer a crushing defeat and separation at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-separated_by_Kuma_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-separated_by_Kuma-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> thus beginning a training period of two years to prepare themselves for the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.</li>
<li>In the 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Moria was ranked 44th, 72nd, 111th, and 74th, respectively.</li>
<li>Moria's teeth were round in his debut chapter, but became fangs from his next appearance onward.</li>
<li>Moria is currently the only known former Warlord of the Sea without a known <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a>.</li>
<li>At 48 years old and 692 cm, Moria is the oldest and tallest individual known to ever hold a position as one of the Seven Warlords of the Sea.</li>
<li>Based on his name, Moria's animal theme is a gecko.<sup id="cite_ref-first_appearance_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first_appearance-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Both parts of his name may support his theme: <i>Gekkō</i> can mean "moonlight"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">月光</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> in Japanese (which suits his horror theme as well) and may also come from the English word gecko, a type of lizard, and "Moria" may come from <i>imori</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">蠑螈</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, "newt")</span> or <i>mori-ao-gaeru</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">モリアオガエル</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, "Forest Green Tree Frog")</span>, since <i>geko</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ゲコ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> is the Japanese onomatopoeia for a frog's croak. And the bolded letters of Gec<b>ko Mori</b>a make <i>komori</i>, which means "bat" in Japanese.</li>
<li>It is also possible that the character's name makes reference to the novel <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Island_of_Doctor_Moreau" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Island of Doctor Moreau"><i>The Island of Dr Moreau</i></a>, by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H.G._Wells" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H.G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, in which a scientist by the name of Doctor Moreau gets stranded on an island and makes experiments, creating monsters by mixing the body parts of animals and men. The similarities between the plot of the novel and the elements of the Thriller Bark arc, along with the similar sounding names of the masters of the islands, seem to confirm the idea that Moria's name is, at least in part, a reference to Moreau.</li></ul></li>
<li>Moria is one of the few characters that keep their unique laugh in the FUNimation dub.</li>
<li>He is the first character who was able to imitate the usage of the <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Gomu Gomu no Mi</a> using a different <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a>. The second and third being <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Charlotte Katakuri</a> using the <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">Mira Mira no Mi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">Mochi Mochi no Mi</a> respectively.
<ul><li>While Brûlée and Katakuri used the techniques themselves, Moria used <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kakumei</a> to manipulate <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>' shadow to perform the attacks.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bentham" title="Bentham">Bentham</a> tried to fool <a href="/wiki/Magellan" title="Magellan">Magellan</a> by using Gomu Gomu no Okama Pistol, Okama Gatling, and Okama Giant Scythe, though he only copied the naming pattern and not the attacks themselves.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the characters description and summary of <a href="/wiki/Volume_47" title="Volume 47">Volume 47</a>, Moria was misidentified as a "former Warlord of the Sea"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">元七武海</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Moto Shichibukai</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> which was inaccurate at the time. However, this never appeared in the actual chapters.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a> English dub, his name is pronounced with a rolled R, likely in reference to the Spanish origins of the name.</li>
<li>Moria is the only known character to be the <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> of two separate crews: the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</a>.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Kibagaeru" title="Kibagaeru">Kibagaeru</a>, the former captain of the <a href="/wiki/Fanged_Toad_Pirates" title="Fanged Toad Pirates">Fanged Toad Pirates</a>, became the captain of the <a href="/wiki/Foxy_Pirates" title="Foxy Pirates">Foxy Pirates</a> in an <a href="/wiki/Foxy%27s_Return_Arc" title="Foxy&#39;s Return Arc">anime-only arc</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Moria's favorite food is marinated caviar.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<li id="cite_note-139"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-139">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga&#32;and Anime — <a href="/wiki/Volume_59" title="Volume 59">Vol. 59</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Chapter_577" title="Chapter 577">Chapter 577</a>&#32;(p. 4)&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_486" title="Episode 486">Episode 486</a>,&#32;Moria sees Whitebeard's standing corpse.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-140"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-140">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga&#32;and Anime — <a href="/wiki/Volume_59" title="Volume 59">Vol. 59</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Chapter_580" title="Chapter 580">Chapter 580</a>&#32;(p. 13-15)&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_489" title="Episode 489">Episode 489</a>,&#32;Moria grins as the war ends.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-141"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-141">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary</a>&#32;(Card #0472),&#32;It is stated that Absalom and Hogback rescued Moria from Doflamingo after the war.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-142"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-142">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/New_World_Times" title="New World Times">New World Times</a> — Witnesses claim to have seen Moria alive.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-143"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-143">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a>&#32;(p. 354),&#32;Early concept of Moria is revealed.</span>
</li>
